Zhejiang Province

[Planning the Construction of the Xiaochang Light Railway]

Cheng Zhenjun, a member of the Zhejiang Provincial Government and Director of the Department of Construction, proposed at the 293rd meeting of the Provincial Government Committee to change the Xiaochang Highway into the Xiaochang Light Railway, requesting a public decision. The proposal was approved. The original proposal is recorded as follows:

"Upon investigation, the Xiaochang Highway is planned to be handled by the Hangzhou-Jiangshan Railway Engineering Bureau of Zhejiang Province, and the section from Xiaoshan to Zhuji will be built first. The Provincial Government Committee has successively proposed and decided this in meetings, and immediately ordered the bureau to comply. The bureau should start construction immediately to comply with the original proposal. However, the entire route is very long, passing through densely populated areas with abundant products. In addition to passenger transport,

it is necessary to take into account freight transport in order to fulfill the main purpose of transportation. After repeated consideration by this department, it is believed that building highways is beneficial for short-distance passenger transport, but uneconomical for long-distance freight and passenger transport. If a railway is built, it would be difficult to raise funds and start construction. After repeated planning, it seems most appropriate to rebuild a light railway, which requires less cost and has broader benefits. The advantages of light railways compared to highways are listed below: (1)

The construction cost of a light railway, including vehicles and equipment, is about 11,000 yuan per *huali* (Chinese mile), while the construction cost of a highway, including vehicles and equipment, is about 8,000 yuan per *huali*. The current cost of various highways is also more than 10,000 yuan. The difference in cost between the two is not significant, but the maintenance cost after the railway is built is very low, and its service life is also longer. (2) The transport capacity of a light railway is larger, with an average of about 400 passengers and 200 tons of goods per train. Highways have smaller carrying capacity and cannot provide long-distance transportation. (3) Railway vehicles are durable, with an average lifespan of 10 to 15 years, while automobiles can only last a maximum of 5 years. (4) The fuel used for railways is coal, and the main materials are steel, both of which can be obtained domestically. The fuel used for automobiles is gasoline, and the main materials are tires, etc., all of which must be purchased from abroad. Furthermore, the Zhengtai narrow-gauge railway is very developed, and the Uekawa Light Railway has also been successfully operated. Others include

Page 12

The light railway of the Liujiang Coal Mine Company, where each train can carry 18 carriages and 180 tons of goods, with each carriage carrying 30 to 40 passengers, is much more convenient than highways. Using that as an example, if the Chang Road can be converted into a light railway, future income will definitely increase. In addition to the budget for this item, which will be proposed separately in the future, this matter concerns a change to an established plan. Is it feasible? It is appropriate to submit a proposal in advance for public decision."

Hunan Provincial Government's Opinions on Land Tax Clearance

▲Advocating for temporary measures first to prepare for fundamental solutions ▲Then gradually improving towards thorough reorganization. Changsha Correspondence: The Ministry of Finance recently approved a letter from the Secretariat of the Central Executive Committee forwarding a request from the Shanghai Special Municipality Executive Committee to the Central Government, requesting the National Government to issue a clear order for a nationwide land tax clearance. It specially copied and forwarded the original request to the Hunan Provincial Government for review and reply. The Hunan Provincial Government yesterday specifically responded in detail on various measures for both temporary and fundamental solutions, for consideration. The reply is as follows: "Regarding the reply, your ministry's letter was approved. The Secretariat of the Central Executive Committee forwarded a submission from the Shanghai Special Municipality Executive Committee, stating that the 11th branch of the 9th district party department under the committee requested to forward to the Central Government a request for the National Government to issue a clear order for a nationwide land tax clearance. The original request was copied and forwarded, instructing review and reply, etc. Upon investigation, the original request considers land tax clearance as an urgent matter to relieve the suffering of the people and enrich the national treasury, which is indeed a profound argument. It also considers land survey as the key to starting clearance, which is also a plan for fundamental solutions.

However, since the Qin and Han dynasties, the beginning of free buying and selling of land opened the door for reclamation and annexation, resulting in private ownership. Repeated changes have created a long history.

Therefore, registers are scattered and untraceable. A sudden land survey cannot be successful overnight. In addition, the military affairs in the Northwest and Western Guangdong have not been settled,

and bandits are rampant in remote border areas. Residents and travelers still lack safety. Moreover, this matter is significant, requiring leaders, surveyors, planning time, handling costs, and legal maintenance. All

these points should be carefully considered and prepared in advance. Hastily attempting it will inevitably lead to waste and little success. This is why this government has repeatedly deliberated and believes that land survey may not be timely until the disbandment has ended and pacification has concluded. However, the tax system has become extremely chaotic today. Knowing that it is impossible but not acting may lead to no hope of success. Therefore, temporary measures must be taken first to prepare for fundamental solutions,

and then gradually improved towards thorough reorganization. The first priority of temporary measures is thorough investigation. The method of thorough investigation is to first dispatch personnel to collect outstanding taxes from each county according to the amount due, with a deadline for collection and remittance. All issues such as less land and more taxes, more land and less taxes, land without taxes, and taxes without land, as well as the true names and addresses of taxpayers, land locations, quantity of land, tax amounts, and different classes should be investigated and recorded in detail during the thorough investigation. Registration forms should be stipulated and separately detailed. It is also necessary to strictly order each county not to deduct cash with grain coupons before raising funds for any item, to avoid deficits and misappropriation, and to limit surcharges to avoid affecting regular supplies. Strictly prohibit contracted collections to prevent clerks from enriching themselves, and prevent free allocations to avoid disrupting tax administration. The above are all positive temporary measures as the first step towards fundamental solutions, which is also what the original request called for: investigation, registration, and price reporting, all of which must be carried out step by step. This government has already included the thorough investigation of land tax and land acreage in its political program and is planning to gradually implement it. However, the accumulated malpractices are too deep, and there are no concrete measures yet. We are eagerly awaiting your ministry's prompt promulgation of good regulations to comply with. Given the previous reasons, we have accordingly expressed our humble opinions for consideration. Please bother to investigate and deal with it. One."

Conclusion of Debate in Xue Diankui Case

Jinan Correspondence: The second hearing of the case against Shou Zhang Xue Diankui for counter-revolution was held at 3 p.m. on the 19th in the Criminal Court No. 1 of the Shandong High Court. Those present included Zhao Zhikui, President of the Criminal Court, judges Li Faxian and Wang Shicheng, prosecutor Liu Zhaofu,

clerk Fang Zhenhua, lawyer Ni Pifang, and many observers from the party department and the press. The questioning proceeded as follows: Court President Zhao Zhikui asked, "Are you Xue Diankui?" Xue answered, "Yes." "How old are you?" "Sixty-four years old." "Where are you from?" "Shou Chang, Henan." "What did you do before?" "Studied." "What were you doing before the crime?" "Chief of the preparatory regiment of the People's Self-Defense Force." "When was the preparatory regiment established?" "It was previously the guard regiment, established in the second year of the Republic of China, and changed to the self-defense force preparatory regiment in the 17th year. Chen Yishen, the commander-in-chief, appointed me as the chief of the entire county." "How many regiments are there in the entire county?" "Fourteen regiments north of the river and ten regiments south of the river." "How many people are in each regiment?" "Thirty or twenty, not equal." "Where does the funding come from?" "Donations are collected from upper, middle, and lower households based on land acreage, also not uniform." "Wasn't your conflict with the party department due to the budget in the 18th year? The police fee in the 18th year was two cents per *mu*, and the regiment fee was one cent and five *li*. Previously, the police fee was five *li* per *mu*, and the regiment fee was one cent. Was the conflict due to this?" "When I was the chief of the regiment, I didn't know about money matters." "Did you oppose the review committee and have disagreements with the party department?" "No." "Did you ever threaten the county magistrate with a gun?" "No." "Did you oppose the party department posting slogans and leaflets? There is evidence to this effect." (He then took out a photo and showed it to Xue Diankui.) "I have never scolded anyone. I don't know about this." "Is it because you have a feud with the party department that they wanted to abolish the regiment chief that the conflict arose?" "No, I am willing to resign, and have resigned several times." "Why resign?" "Because the farmers' association was established, and the two rascals Ge Panqin and Ge Wensheng intervened. I resigned for fear of accidents." "Do you oppose the Kuomintang?" "I don't oppose it." "Why did you conflict with the party department on July 9th?" "Wu, the district chief of Linqing, sent a letter

inviting me to Linqing for a meeting to discuss joint defense against bandits. I went to the yamen to see the county magistrate and on the way back, I encountered Han and Li from the party department under a locust tree in Xiaoyushou. They asked if I was carrying a gun. I replied that I was not carrying a gun. The two soldiers were also not carrying guns. Han and Li each carried a pistol and a Mauser." "Why were Han and Li wounded by gunfire?" "At this time, I had already passed by in front. They quarreled with my guards, and the guards snatched the gun." "Did you teach him to shoot?" "No, it was a misfire." "You don't need to prevaricate. A policeman saw and heard you teach him to shoot." "No, if I taught him to shoot, it would not have been just one shot. I even forbade him." "Did the county magistrate inspect after the shooting?" "Yes." "How did they attack the city later?" "Ge Panqin and Ge Wensheng left the city and invited the Red Spear Society to attack the city. These two were wanted by the Civil Affairs Department." "Were you in the city when the city was attacked, directing the shooting?" "No shots were fired in the city." "Where were they outside the city?" "They gathered more than 1,000 people near Nantai outside the city and drove away the original Nantai Self-Defense Force preparatory regiment." "How was Cai Guanghan, the chief of the regiment, kidnapped by them?" "Cai was the chief of the second regiment. Because he was old, he left the city to visit home and was kidnapped by them on the way through Nantai." "What happened later?" "The county magistrate sent the chief of the public security bureau and the president of the court to mediate twice. I even said that as long as Cai Guanghan was released, any conditions could be agreed to. They ultimately refused." "How did the men under Cai's command get to Tainan later? Did you teach them to go?" "No, his guards were eager to save their master and invited people to go." "How many people went?" "Thirty to forty people, mostly guards. They went on the evening of the tenth." "What was the result?" "Hou Zhaojin, a regiment member who went, was killed by them, and Cai Guanghan was beaten and hanged. He died after being rescued. Regiment member Xue Hongxun was killed while defending the city." "Who killed Shi Jiuqing, the secretary of the Farmers' Association Anti-Japanese Association and secretary of the party department, and four others?" "I don't know." "Was it because your relationship with the party department was too bad, and it became more intense after Han came out?"

"I dare not be intense." "How do you feel about the Kuomintang?" "Welcome. I was a member of the Kuomintang in the first year of the Republic of China and worked with Zhang Ruixuan. He was a friend of Sun Yat-sen. I also donated money when the party department was established." "Why is your relationship with the party department so bad?" "The party department was fooled by Ge Panqin and Ge Wensheng.

These two are rebels and bad people. They have now been expelled from the party.

Chairman Chen once arrested the two of them and Shen, the director of the Construction Bureau." "Do you oppose the Three Principles of the People?" "I don't oppose it. I am a member of the Min Party." At this point, the court president ordered Xue Diankui to step down and invited lawyer Ni Pifang to express his opinion. Ni stood up and said, "This case has been reviewed by your court for many days, and the questioning today has also been clarified. Please ask the prosecutor to express his opinion." Prosecutor Liu Zhaofu stood up and said,

"The details of this case have been stated clearly in the indictment. However, what Xue Diankui actually thinks of the Kuomintang is a question that must be paid attention to in order to determine whether or not he is a counter-revolutionary. Furthermore, it is necessary to pay attention to whether or not Xue Diankui has a feud with Ge Panqin and Ge Wensheng. Also, Xue Diankui should be responsible for the fact that five people were killed by the regiment members when he was the chief of the regiment." At this point, the court president asked Xue Diankui again, "Is your relationship with the party department bad?" "Not bad, I often go to the party department." "Do you oppose Ge Panqin and Ge Wensheng, or do you oppose the Kuomintang?"

"Oppose the two Ges, not the Kuomintang." "Did you fire guns in the city when they were fighting outside the city?" "No shots were fired in the city." At this point, the clerk read the confession and ordered Xue to sign it in court. Finally, Xue Diankui was asked again, "Do you have anything else to say?" "In short, I don't hate the party department." The court declared the debate in this case concluded and scheduled a date for sentencing, and then adjourned. (February 19)

Mo Dehui Passes Through Tianjin to Return to Shenyang

Tianjin Correspondence: Mo Dehui, the superintendent of the Chinese Eastern Railway, was summoned to Beijing last month to discuss issues with Russia. After completing his affairs, he returned north. When he arrived in Jinan, Chen Tiaoyuan provided a special train for him to travel north. (Yesterday, the 18th) He left Jinan at 2:30 a.m. and arrived at Tianjin East Station around 9 p.m. The Public Security Bureau and the Garrison Command sent teams and bands to welcome him at the station. Garrison Commander Chuan Zuoyi and Brigade Commander Yuan Qingzeng also arrived at the station to welcome him. After the train stopped, Mo briefly mingled with the welcomers and then took Commander Chuan's car to Chuan's residence for dinner. Those traveling with him

included Wu Zesheng and Cai Yunchen, the Secretary-General of the Eastern Route. Mo's entourage of eleven people also got off the train and transferred to a chartered carriage provided by the Beining Railway, attached to the No. 105 passenger train to Shenyang. A reporter met Mo at Chuan's residence and asked about the central government's current policy towards Russia and the Northeast authorities' handling of the negotiations. Mo's remarks were as follows: "The central government's policy towards the Eastern Route has been declared by the Ministry of Foreign Affairs. Some clauses in the draft agreement of the Khabarovsk Conference exceed the scope of discussion.

Therefore, the current dispute is over the Eastern Route, and the representative authority of Cai Yunsheng is also limited to discussing the scope of the Eastern Route. Other general Sino-Russian issues are beyond Cai's authority to discuss, and the Northeast authorities have no power to resolve them. Therefore, the central government has declared that it does not recognize the draft agreement signed by Cai beyond his authority, except for those pertaining to the Eastern Route. The Russian goal is also to restore the Eastern Route to its state before July, and they should not invoke the draft agreement and make other demands.

Therefore, since the Ministry of Foreign Affairs' declaration was issued, the Russians have not had any reaction. This is because the national spirit of our country cannot be humiliated, and the international community would also not approve. The central government has appointed me to go to Russia this time to attend the meeting. I tried my best to decline, but due to my responsibilities, I could not help but force myself to do so. I will use my loyalty to the country and a fearless spirit to negotiate. If the Russians make any threats, I will never yield. The authority granted to me by the central government is also limited to discussing the Eastern Route issue, that is, to continue and

resolve the problem by seeking to continue implementing the Sino-Russian Fengtian Agreement. The Fengtian Agreement stipulates that our country can unconditionally recover the Eastern Route after sixty years, and can also redeem it at a price before the deadline. However, how to evaluate it and how to pay for it, and whether it can be redeemed with bonds, will all be discussed at this meeting. Also, before the redemption, a most fair method of joint management should be discussed to avoid further disputes. This dispute was caused by unfairness. If the Russians want to avoid future disputes, they should be happy to discuss joint management methods with us. After I return to Liaoning, I still have to go to Harbin to handle various matters, and I will not be able to depart for Russia until mid-March. Experts sent by the Ministry of Foreign Affairs and the Ministry of Railways will also travel with me for consultation. The Northeast authorities have worked hard to deal with the Eastern Route issue this time. They know that the strength of the Northeast is not enough to

oppose the strength of Russia, but forced to fight for the face of the country and the personality of the nation, they had to send troops to resist the enemy. However, the country is becoming more and more difficult, internal wars are breaking out one after another, and a certain country is trying to take the opportunity to stir up trouble. The 100,000 troops of the Eastern Province have been exposed for half a year, and public and private losses are difficult to estimate. The Russian bandits are deepening their penetration, and more than ten counties along the border have been ravaged by them, and they are about to cross the Xing'an Mountains to the east. A Soviet government has been organized in Hulunbuir. The South Allied Mongolian Youth League wants to communize various places in Manzhouli. The people of various counties along the border are crying out for help, asking the authorities to resolve the dispute as soon as possible. Therefore, there was the initial consultation in Shuangchengzi. At that time, it was reported that the Russians were demanding compensation for military expenses from our side,

and stationed troops to protect the railway. Fortunately, this did not materialize, so there was the Khabarovsk meeting. Although Cai Yunsheng made some mistakes, if you think back to the difficulties at the time, there are many things that can be understood. Those who do not know the content are only demanding on paper, which is far from the facts. Now that the central government has denied a part of it, it is enough to remedy it," and so on. Mo and his party left Tianjin at 12 p.m. last night on the Tongpu Railway,

and Commander Chuan and others still went to the station to see them off in person. (19th)

Liaoning Province Rectifies the Judiciary

Shenyang Correspondence: Liaoning Provincial Government member Liu Heling and others recently proposed to rectify the judiciary in the province and drafted six measures. The 91st meeting of the Provincial Committee approved the proposal and reported it to the Northeast Political Affairs Committee for instructions. The Political Affairs Committee has now instructed that it be filed for record. The original proposal and measures are excerpted as follows: (1) Supervise personnel administration. The appointment and removal of judicial officials should be handled in accordance with regulations. The Provincial Government has the power to supervise the judiciary. In the future, the appointment, removal, or transfer of local court presidents, chief procurators, ordinary prosecutors, and clerks should be reported to the Provincial Government by the High Court and the relevant department for verification.

Those who have been appointed or transferred in the past should also be investigated and reported by the court for approval in accordance with the procedures. (2) Investigate courts and prisons. Recently, local courts in the province have been slow, biased, and prone to bribery and solicitation in handling civil and criminal cases. Therefore, there have been many cases of people complaining to the government. Prisons and detention centers definitely engage in arbitrary extortion of prisoners and prolonged detention without resolution. People outside are talking about it. If this is not actively rectified, it will lead to criticism both internally and externally.

The High Court and its Procuratorate should be instructed to thoroughly rectify the situation. At the same time, the Provincial Government should appoint personnel familiar with judicial and prison administration to go to various places to conduct thorough investigations for verification and handling. (3) Strictly prohibit manipulation of sentences. In criminal cases, the principal penalty is broad. Judges should use their conscience to determine the sentence and must not manipulate it based on private intentions to avoid suspicion of breaking the law. The High Court and the Procuratorate should be instructed to strictly investigate their subordinates. If anyone loses or gains in criminal cases, they should be immediately subject to disciplinary action. If anyone intentionally manipulates it, they should be prosecuted for dereliction of duty under Article 133 of the Criminal Law. (4) Maintain judges' salaries. Judges have complex affairs,

and their salaries have always been low, which is not enough to reward them and cultivate their integrity. The High Court and its Procuratorate should be instructed to give priority to judges' and clerks' salaries within the budget scope and not to reduce or delay payment. All judicial surplus funds should not be used to add new agencies for the time being, but should first be used to actively rectify existing courts and prisons to avoid simply expanding and increasing the name while actually being perfunctory and exhausted. (5) Report judicial income and expenditure. The Provincial Government has no record of how much of the provincial judicial expenses are supplemented by judicial income in addition to the fixed amount of 200,000 yuan from the province each year, and what the total judicial income is for the year. The High Court and its Procuratorate should be instructed to prepare a detailed statement of the annual income for verification to clarify the situation. In the future, if there is a surplus in judicial income, it should not be requested to be retained unless there is an urgent need to show restriction. (6) Remove restrictions on the number of lawyers. The number of lawyers in this province has always been limited (about 50), which is unreasonable. The number is very small, which is enough to create a special opportunity for lawyers within the quota, resulting in extortion and monopoly, and litigants feel quite painful. The High Court and the Procuratorate should be instructed to remove this prohibition, allowing lawyers to register and operate freely at any time. However, if anyone does not abide by the rules of lawyers, the chief procurator of each locality should be instructed to strictly investigate and punish them. If there are any lawyers who secretly collude with judges, the judges should be punished,

otherwise, the responsible official will be held accountable. (17th)

Guangdong Provincial Civil and Education Department Heads Take Office

▲Chen Mingshu presided over the oath and delivered a speech. Guangzhou Correspondence: Since Zeng Jian, the provincial committee member and director of the Civil Affairs Department, resigned from all his concurrent positions, the central government immediately issued an order appointing Huang Jusu as a member of the provincial government, Xu Chongqing, the former member of the provincial committee, as the director of the Civil Affairs Department, and Jin Zengcheng as the director of the Education Department. After the three received their letters of appointment, they took office in the provincial government today (15th). The meeting was held at around 8 a.m. After the newly appointed provincial committee member Huang Jusu, Civil Affairs Department Director Xu Chongqing, and Education Department Director Jin Zengcheng took their oaths in turn, the oath-taking official Chen Mingshu delivered a speech, saying, "Today I represent the central government to deliver a speech to the three of you. But the three of you are all comrades who are familiar to me. The speech is always the same, so there is nothing to say. As for the three of you, everyone knows about your party history and work, so there is no need to introduce you again. The three of you are far superior to me in learning and talent. It is a happy thing that you can all come to serve Guangdong today. As for myself, since taking over provincial affairs, I originally wanted to immediately build Guangdong into a model province, but things did not go as planned. In the past year, wars have repeatedly broken out in the province, so that all the strength of the provincial government has been directed towards military affairs, and no construction projects can be implemented. I am truly sorry. Now that the enemies have been destroyed to some extent, they have not yet been completely eliminated. Fortunately, the war has shifted to Guangxi. However, due to historical and economic relations between the two Guangs, Guangdong cannot be at peace unless Guangxi is settled. Therefore, the current government is still working hard on military affairs, hoping that the military affairs in Guangxi will end soon. The sooner the military affairs in Guangxi end, the sooner the construction of Guangdong will be realized. I hope everyone understands this. The people should fully assist the government in resolving the Guangxi issue. The people of Guangdong are inherently creative. If the military affairs end, it is expected that there will be remarkable construction projects. The people and the government should be of one mind and work towards one goal in today's environment to accomplish the great mission for the party and the country," and so on. After the speech, Huang, Xu, and Jin each gave a reply. The meeting adjourned at around 11 a.m. It is heard that Director Jin has already taken office and started work today, while Director Xu is scheduled to start work at the Civil Affairs Department on the 17th. February 15 evening)

Local Correspondence

Suzhou

The Pudong gang robbed two towns in one day. The towns of Nanbeiqiao and Weijing, under the jurisdiction of the county, were robbed by a gang of 60 to 70 bandits from Pudong at 11 a.m. on the 21st, who arrived in 13 boats. The bandits were all armed with Mauser pistols and fast rifles. They immediately robbed more than ten shops, including Tang Dongmao's shop, and stole the guns from the water police boats stationed in the town. At the same time, the bandits spread out as sentries around the town, firing guns to intimidate and kill one person and wound two people, including water police inspector Li Liang.

The robbery lasted for four hours, and the bandits then took the loot and boarded the boats, heading towards Yangcheng Lake. Yesterday, the sixth police station of the county public security bureau reported the incident to the county public security bureau and then reported it to the county government. The gang also robbed the town of Wutangjing after robbing Weijingtang Town. They landed at about 6 p.m. and used Mauser pistols to intimidate the 11th outpost of the public security bureau. The reserve policeman Li Yunqing was shot and injured. The outpost was unable to resist due to insufficient strength.

The bandits then split up and robbed for about an hour before taking the loot and boarding the boats, heading towards Yangcheng Lake again. The total monetary loss is about 10,000 yuan. The Wu County Government and the 3rd District of the Water Public Security Bureau have dispatched teams to the countryside to pursue the bandits after receiving the report.

Kunshan

A stray bullet caused death, requesting a pension. Fang, the wife of Yu Jiang, a migrant from Chongming living in Zhang Jinqiao, Luxia Township, was struck in the left armpit by a stray bullet while soldiers of the army stationed at the station were practicing target shooting in front of the Land Temple at 9 a.m. on January 30. Zhang Yilun, the director of the Second District, went to the township to inspect the scene and provided 20 yuan for medical expenses.

He also sent a police inspector from the public security bureau to accompany her to Shanghai Guangren Hospital for treatment. She died in the hospital on the 19th due to her serious injuries. After Yu received the news, he claimed the body and prepared the coffin. However, because his family is extremely poor and he has two young children who are still breastfeeding, he requested Director Zhang to grant a pension to help him make a living. After receiving the request, Director Zhang has written to the officer in charge of the team to consider granting it. It is not known whether his wish will be fulfilled.

Jiading

Lost After Drunkenness at a Wedding Feast: Zhu Liusheng's two sons, Jinquan, aged 16, and Yinbao, aged 13, from Zhu Family Residence, Anting Township, under this county, attended a wedding feast at a neighboring village on the evening before last (the 20th). They drank too much and staggered home. However, Zhu waited until dawn but the two sons did not return home. He asked at the Zhang family's residence, and was told that they had left together at ten o'clock. Zhu became extremely anxious, fearing they had accidentally fallen into the river and drowned after getting drunk. He searched the river everywhere but found no trace.

National Walking Group Passes Through Jiading: Zhou Changsheng, Xu Yintang, Liang Daxin, Jiang Xisheng, Liu Hanru, Lou Junxia and other six members of the National Walking Group, departed from the Shanghai North Railway Station on the 20th and walked to Nanxiang Town under this county on the same day. On the 21st, they came to the city of Jiading and visited the County Government, the Education Association, and the Construction Bureau to conduct inspections and investigations. They brought a camera and filmed scenes such as the Tan Ying Pavilion in the park. They left Jiading for Taicang this morning.

Yesterday and today, he went to the Anting, Huangdu, Sixth and Seventh District Offices to convene township chiefs and deputies, inquiring in detail about the agricultural conditions of each district.

It is said that he must travel throughout all districts of the county. A Hired Maid Runs Away Wearing Her Employer's Clothes: A Yu family in West Main Street in the city hired a young woman named A Mei, an adopted daughter-in-law with the surname Xiang, as a domestic helper. A Mei was only eighteen years old, and her husband worked as a plasterer. They did not look good together and their relationship was strained. The day before yesterday, A Mei stole and put on her employer's leather qipao and velvet rope hat, and secretly ran away. The detective team has now been notified to investigate.

Qingpu

An Old Man Catches Adultery but Ends up a Married Couple: A certain Ma, a resident of Qingpu under a certain town who came from Jiangbei, is now 24 years old. Six years ago, she married Feng Xiaoqing, who was from the same village, through a matchmaker. Three years after the marriage, Xiaoqing died of illness, leaving behind an elderly mother and a son. Xiaoqing had an elder brother named Daqing, who is now working as a coolie in a certain rice mill. His income is very meager, so it is difficult for him to take care of the elderly mother and the widowed sister-in-law. Ma had no means of making a living, so she became acquainted with a clerk named Kuang in a certain store. All daily expenses were provided by Kuang. The day before yesterday, Daqing asked Kuang for some money for his elderly mother's old age expenses, but Kuang refused. Daqing then discovered the night before last that Kuang was spending the night at his sister-in-law's place, so he gathered a group of people and went to catch them in adultery, capturing the adulterous couple. Later, after mediation by Daqing's mother and Kuang's relatives and friends, Kuang paid one hundred yuan to subsidize the elderly mother for the rest of her life. Ma formally married Kuang, and the three-year-old child was raised by Daqing. The matter ended there.

A Wife Deceives Her Husband and Runs Away with Belongings to Her Parents' Home: Xu Mengsheng, a villager from Xucun Township in Qingpu, is 28 years old. He married Ma Xiulai's daughter through a matchmaker two years ago. After the marriage, the couple's relationship was not bad. However, since the autumn of last year, his wife often liked to go out. Xu, being weak by nature, did not stop her. On December 22nd last year, his wife suddenly told her husband that she needed to spend the Lunar New Year with her mother's family and would return after the Lantern Festival in the first month. Xu believed it to be true and let her go to her parents' home. The day before yesterday, the husband went to his parents-in-law's house to inquire, but Xiulai said that she had not returned to their home. Xu then returned home to check his trunks, only to find that all his clothes and ornaments were gone. Xu suddenly realized that his wife had run away with his belongings. He is now searching everywhere.

County Government Ordered to Prepare for the Establishment of a Granary: The granary established in this county has been virtually eliminated since the founding of the Republic of China. Therefore, there is only the name of the granary, but not the reality. Now the county government has received an order from the Civil Affairs Department of Jiangsu Province to establish a granary, and has issued organizational regulations. After receiving the order, County Magistrate Shen has sent a letter to the Property Department, urging them to quickly prepare for the establishment of a granary to emphasize famine relief.

Minutes of the Standing Committee Meeting of the National Federation of Private Electric Power Companies: On the 20th of this month, the National Federation of Private Electric Power Companies held a standing committee meeting in Nanjing. It was resolved that the association should send representatives to attend, and the selection of representatives will be decided at the next meeting. The travel expenses are limited to 5,000 yuan, which will be raised by the association. The proposal to convene a meeting of the entire executive and supervisory committee was resolved to be held on April 5th. All committee members will be notified immediately to attend at that time.

which had previously been revised by the county government after convening a meeting of both parties, was submitted to the Department of Construction for review. Legal Entities Supervise the Handover of the Finance Bureau: Fang Jingzhong, the director of the Jiangdu Finance Bureau, stated that the numbers in the handover case during Chen Fang's tenure were still in line, but regarding local expenses, legal entities should supervise the calculation in accordance with regulations. Yesterday (20th), letters were specifically sent to the County Chamber of Commerce, the Education Bureau, the Public Security Bureau, and other bureaus, asking them to send representatives to the bureau at 2:00 p.m. on the 21st for supervision. the numbers were still consistent, and they have separately stamped their seals for reporting purposes.

Yangguan Announces the Registration of Treasury Bonds: Yanghai Customs issued a notice to all merchants, instructing those who hold treasury bonds compiled by the customs to go to the customs to register their numbers before August 30th in order to receive a 2% rebate. The Yi and Liang Roads are Scheduled to Start Construction: The Construction Bureau complied with the provincial order to first construct the Yangyi and Yangliang roads. Funing

Joint Patrol of Police Teams from Two Counties: County Magistrate Xiao of Yancheng, due to the frequent movement of bandits in the Caoniankou area bordering Yancheng and Funing, made a telephone appointment with the Funing County Police Team yesterday to conduct a joint patrol there at 4:00 p.m. today (17th). Industry Police Team Killed a Bandit: Li Guangcai, the fourth squad leader of the second brigade of the special police team of the Taihaiqi Industry stationed in Qianqiugang in the eastern part of this county, encountered a bandit yesterday in the Nanjian Duikan area and killed the bandit on the spot, whose name is unknown. A business card was found in the pocket of the bandit's clothes, which read Zhou Yushan, with Yanqing Su written next to it.

A pistol was also found, and a hostage, Sun Hanmin, was rescued. However, the hostage's foot was injured by a stray bullet and has now been taken back by his family for treatment.

Jointly Request Relief Funds: In recent years, this county has suffered heavily from brine backflow and locust plagues, resulting in severe disaster conditions. Now that the spring plowing season is approaching, the disaster victims have neither food nor seeds for planting. All party and government agencies and organizations jointly submitted a request to the provincial agencies and the Shanghai Chinese and Foreign Famine Relief Committee, the China Jisheng Society, and the Funing Shanghai Temporary Disaster Relief Association today (18th), requesting the prompt allocation of funds for relief and the issuance of large quantities of seeds to avoid the worry of having fields but no seeds to plant.

Gaoyou

Establishing Telephones in the Four Villages: Jia Chengchun, the director of the Construction Bureau of this county, in order to facilitate communication in the four villages of this county, plans to establish telephones in the four villages, which requires an estimated cost of more than 10,000 yuan. San Duo to Linze is the first phase, and the rest will be established successively. Once approved by the Department of Construction, work will begin.

Xue Zi Kidnapped: The family of farmer Xue Wenyi in Shangcun, Qili, Wuzong, under this county,

was suddenly visited by five bandits at 8:00 p.m. the night before last. Each of them was armed with guns and spoke with a northern accent. After entering, they tied up the Xue couple and burned Xue's nose with fire, interrogating them about hidden silver. A considerable amount of clothing and cash was robbed. Before leaving, they also kidnapped Xue's son. They have now come to the city to report to the county government and request a strict investigation.

Jiaxing

The Customs Bureau Invites Merchants to Contract the Silk Tax: The silk tax of the Jiaxing Customs Bureau, especially the silk tax of Xinwang Jiangjing, is contracted by merchant Shen Tianjue. Now, due to the decline of the silk industry, Shen Tianjue explained that he would withdraw from the contract when the contract period expired on February 20th. After the director of the Customs Bureau, Jiang Zhicheng, reported to the Department of Finance for review, he still planned to invite merchants to bid for the contract. The bidding methods are: (1) The minimum annual contract amount is tentatively set at 7,000 yuan; (2) The bidding period is from February 23rd to February 27th; (3) The bidding will be opened at 2:00 p.m. on February 28th.

County Government Prepares Zoning Plan: The Jiaxing zoning conference has been convened by the county government three times, but it has not been resolved. The fourth zoning conference is scheduled to be convened today (23rd) in the Zhongshan Hall in the city, with the village chiefs and heads of villages attending. It is learned that the county government, in order to facilitate the resolution,

has submitted a request to the Department of Civil Affairs to assume the number of zones. It was approved to temporarily limit it to seven zones. Therefore, the county government has now formulated four plans:

(1) Five zones; (2) Six zones; (3) Seven zones; (4) Divided according to the current police zones. These proposed plans will be submitted for discussion at today's meeting.

Huzhou

Bandits Intercept and Rob, Shooting Two People: In Kanglin, at the border of the three counties of Wuxing, Wukang, and Anji under Huzhou, at around 8:00 p.m. the day before yesterday, four people from Anji, including Ye Quanmao and Wang Kef, were returning home from Wukang. On the way, they suddenly encountered six bandits speaking with a Hakka accent, who blocked their way. They took out pistols and searched the four people, robbing them of more than 90 yuan and stripping off their clothes. They also shot and wounded Wang Kef and Ye Quanmao. After the robbery, they went east.

Residents Repel Bandits: Tang Caibao, a resident of Yuhong Village in the southeastern part of this city, is quite wealthy. Recently, due to the rampant banditry, Tang spent money to hire many workers to guard day and night, and purchased several shotguns to prevent accidents. Unexpectedly, on the evening of the 18th, eight bandits speaking with a Henan accent and holding guns suddenly came and used stones to break down the door. Tang knew something was wrong and gathered his family members, each holding weapons, and rushed out. Seeing the situation was not good, the bandits retreated to an open field. The two sides clashed and fought for half an hour. The bandits were finally defeated and fled in a southwest direction.

Hangzhou

Lottery Drawing at the Electric Plant Entertainment Cinema: The Hangzhou Electric Plant User Entertainment Cinema, in order to treat the audience who pre-purchased tickets and arouse interest in electrical appliances, has decided to hold a lottery drawing every day from 9:00 a.m. to 1:00 p.m. starting today. Those who hold the lottery tickets attached to the tickets can go to supervise the lottery drawing as scheduled. The first prize is an electric fan, the second prize is an electric hot pot, and the third to eighth prizes are electric heating appliances and theater tickets of great value.

Zhuji

Local Tyrant Cuts His Cousins: In Zhuqiao, outside the North Gate of Zhuji, the notorious local tyrant Lu Junfu is usually extremely overbearing. Recently, his direct cousin Lu Changlai from the same village went to cut firewood on his own mountain the day before yesterday. The local tyrant led many of his henchmen to surround Changlai and beat him severely. He also used a wood knife to slash Changlai's head, causing a wound more than three inches deep. Blood flowed all over the ground, and he was barely breathing and on the verge of death. After the incident, Changlai was carried to the county court to examine the injury and filed a complaint requesting a strict investigation in accordance with the law.

The Traffic Between Hefei and Lu'an is Blocked Due to Bandits: Bandits are rampant in Jinqiao, Guanting, Maji, and Yuji areas on the border of Hefei and Lu'an, robbing, kidnapping, and intercepting passersby, making travelers fear the road and blocking traffic. Local News

French Representative Signed the Shanghai Court Agreement Yesterday

The revised Shanghai Court Agreement has been formally signed with five countries: Britain, the United States, the Netherlands, Portugal, and Brazil. The French representative had not signed it due to not receiving instructions from the French ambassador, and the signing was delayed. Recently, the French Consul General, Gauthier, received instructions and immediately notified the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to schedule the supplementary signing in Shanghai yesterday.

Yesterday morning at 11:00, Xu Mo, the Director of the European and American Department of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, representing China, and Consul General Gauthier, representing France, held a formal supplementary signing ceremony in the Shanghai office of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs. After both parties signed, they shook hands happily and dispersed.

The Norwegian Minister is scheduled to go to Beijing tonight, and will present his credentials tomorrow. The office has notified the Railway Bureau to prepare a decorated car. Japanese Chargé d'Affaires Continued to Visit Foreign Minister Wang Yesterday

▲Shigemitsu Said that Sino-Japanese Negotiations Will Not Be Suspended After Foreign Minister Wang arrived in Shanghai the day before yesterday, Japanese Chargé d'Affaires Shigemitsu Aoi visited him. Heavy Fog Disrupts Shipping

▲Imported Vessels All Halted: On the 21st night of this city, a heavy fog suddenly descended. The waterways outside the Wusong port were even more shrouded in mist, making it impossible to discern the routes. Shanghai-bound outgoing vessels were all anchored within Sanxia Water to avoid danger. As for the north-south liners expected to arrive in Shanghai, such as Tianjin Maru, Tongzhou, Lushan Maru, and Sichuan No. 4, a total of six ships were anchored en route, daring not to proceed. Even Yangtze River steamers like Daji Maru, Wusong, and Ruihe dared not sail. Numerous foreign vessels also preemptively anchored to take refuge. Therefore, only the Ningbo-bound Xin Jiangtian and Ningxing vessels entered the port yesterday. Last night, the fog became even denser. After 6:30 PM, the Huangpu River resembled a sea of mist, making it difficult to distinguish anything just inches away. Although the Shanghai-Ningbo vessels that departed from Shanghai that day had already set sail, they mostly anchored at the Wusong port to the sea, continuously sounding their horns throughout the night. It is feared that all the merchant vessels previously blocked will have difficulty entering the port today, and transportation on the rivers and seas will be disrupted.

▲Accident of Japanese Fishing Boats: Recently, Japanese fishing boats have frequently crossed the border to fish in our waters, which not only hinders our fishing industry but also infringes upon our maritime rights. On the 25th of last month, two more Japanese fishing boats, one called Baoyang Maru and the other called Fengpu Maru, each with a carrying capacity of 19 tons, departed from Shimonoseki and went directly to Wusongkou, China, to fish. However, on the 26th, they encountered a strong wind and fog. In the area of Jeju Island, the two ships were separated by the waves. Baoyang Maru sent a wireless message to Shimonoseki, inquiring about the whereabouts of Fengpu Maru. Starting from the 27th, the wind became even stronger and the fog denser.

Baoyang Maru was battered by wind and waves to a point 70 miles away from Huabiao Island. The crew's calls for help went unanswered. The hull was damaged, and the rudder was broken. All food could not be cooked. The crew members drifted on the ship for four days and nights. Finally, on the 7th of this month, they were spotted by a Chinese cargo ship, which rescued the Japanese captain Yu Cun Bing Shi and crew members Shi Jin, Shan Gang, and Zhai Teng, providing them with food and clothing. They have now been brought to Shanghai. According to the ship owner Yu Cun, there were five Japanese crew members on board the Fengpu Maru, and they are likely to have perished. Furthermore, the hull of Baoyang Maru has also broken and sunk into the sea.

▲Situation at Wusong Port: Yesterday morning, at dawn, a heavy fog suddenly arose at Wusong Port, filling the sky. The sea lanes at Sanxia Water were indistinguishable. Merchant ships sailing from Shanghai could not proceed after reaching Song. For a time, the sounds of horns and bells were incessant. The ships had to anchor temporarily. The nautical lighthouse at Baotai Mountain temporarily shone its light to prevent accidents for incoming ships. Due to the east-west and south stone reefs that cross the Huangpu River in Songkou, navigation is even more dangerous. At around 12:00 noon, a sailboat also encountered fog, lost its way, and accidentally struck a stone reef, causing it to capsize. Fortunately, all the crew members were able to climb ashore. In the afternoon, the fog became even denser, so incoming merchant ships could not enter Songkou and had to berth at Sanxia Water. As dusk fell, the fog was still all over the sky. According to shipping experts, such heavy fog is unprecedented in recent times.

Reiteration of Nighttime Curfew Order

Due to the unrest in the city last winter, the military and police authorities announced a temporary curfew, cutting off traffic after 12:00 midnight every night. Later, due to the end of the lunar year and the frequent travels of business collectors, the restriction on traffic was implicitly relaxed to show consideration.

Counting the days, it has been more than two weeks since then, and the city has been as peaceful as usual. Now, because Taiyuan's Yan (Xishan) has issued a telegram, rumors are rife. The military and police authorities must strive to maintain local security. Starting from the day before yesterday, double posts have been added to all roads in the Chinese areas every night after 6:00 PM. Armed police officers are stationed in rotation at the borders between the Chinese and concession areas, with three to five officers at each location. Detectives and female inspectors are also cooperating to inspect pedestrians and vehicles at key points to prevent unforeseen circumstances. Every night at 12:00, traffic is cut off according to the curfew law. No one is allowed to pass without a password or symbol.

Aviation Administration

Transfer of Hongqiao Aircraft to Beijing: The Hongqiao Airport received an order from the Aviation Administration of the Ministry of Military Affairs yesterday, ordering the transfer of six aircraft to Beijing. Three of them will depart today. The remaining aircraft will also be able to fly to Beijing within days after inspection. The pilots are all assigned by the Aviation Administration and sent to Shanghai.

Tianjin-Pukou Railway Transfers 50 Cars

▲Railway Orders Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway Bureau to Send Cars: The Tianjin-Pukou Railway Bureau, in view of the current shortage of vehicles on the line and the heavy volume of passenger and freight transport, specially requested the Ministry of Railways a few days ago to allocate 50 cars from the Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway for temporary use. The Ministry of Railways has approved this request and telegraphed the Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway Bureau to collect and send the cars to Beijing to cross the river as soon as possible to meet the urgent need.

Change of Directors of Two Railway Bureaus

▲Hu Jixian Returns to the Ministry to Serve: ▲Liu Weizhi to Take Over Tomorrow: Hu Jixian, Director of the Finance Department of the Ministry of Railways and concurrently in charge of the affairs of the Beijing-Shanghai and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway Administrations, received an order from the Ministry of Railways yesterday to return to the Ministry to serve. Liu Weizhi, Director of the Business Department of the Ministry, has been specially appointed to concurrently manage the affairs of the two railways. After receiving the order, Hu has instructed all departments and sections to rush to complete the handover. It is learned that Liu is scheduled to come to the bureau tomorrow (Monday) to take over.

Reorganization of the General Affairs Department of Two Railway Bureaus

The General Affairs Department of the Beijing-Shanghai and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railways originally had seven sections: Documentation, Compilation and Investigation,

Communications, Land Affairs, General Affairs, Police Affairs, and Personnel. The Personnel Section has now been abolished. It is rumored that the Compilation and Investigation Section will also be merged into the Documentation Section, and a new Health Section will be established.

Min Sniper Case

▲Instigated by Lin Shouchang: The Shanghai Naval Reorganization Office received a telegram yesterday from Chen Jiliang, Commander of the First Fleet, from Fujian, stating that the recent sniper attack by thugs on Zhang Yuejun's adjutant Li Zhonghang and the driver, resulting in serious injuries, was carried out by a perpetrator named Ni Shanqi, who was captured after being wounded. All others escaped. The provincial government has offered a reward of 5,000 yuan for their arrest. According to Ni's confession, the instigator was Lin Shouchang. It is said that Lin is one of the most disruptive individuals in Fujian, hence this desperate measure.

Party Department Opposes Jin-Yan

▲Declaration of the First District Party Department: The Executive Committee of the First District Party Department of this city yesterday declared its opposition to Yan Xishan's absurd remarks, saying, "Mr. Yan Baichuan's advocacy of 'courtesy and concession as the way to govern the country' is a fundamental betrayal of the Party and the principles. There is absolutely no room for courtesy and concession from a revolutionary standpoint. Revolution is our duty and our obligation. What courtesy and concession is there to talk about? As for enjoying rights, that can indeed be done with courtesy and concession. It seems that Mr. Yan himself is specializing in enjoying rights without fulfilling obligations in North China. Mr. Yan Baichuan's advocacy that national affairs should be resolved by the people of the country and party affairs should be resolved by the people of the party is a fundamental destruction of the Party's proposition of building the country with the Party and governing the country with the Party. It seems that he wants to eliminate the Party and bring out the Senate to replay the farce of separatism and strife of the past seventeen years, unconditionally offering the entire Chinese territory and people to the hands of imperialism. Mr. Yan Baichuan's proposal to jointly resolve national affairs by uniting the first, second, and third Executive and Supervisory Committees is a fundamental violation of the constitution and is extremely absurd. In short, Mr. Yan Baichuan, holding an important position, does not strive to work on the great path of revolutionary construction and the aspects of protecting the country and securing the people, but instead is wholeheartedly using speculative means to undermine peaceful unification, endanger the Party and the country, and is willing to be a traitor to the principles and a public enemy of the people, taking his own destruction and following in the footsteps of Tang Shengzhi and Feng Yuxiang. All comrades in this district, for the sake of removing revolutionary obstacles, will engage in hand-to-hand combat with the counter-revolutionary feudal forces, and will never give up until the goal of thoroughly eliminating the feudal forces is achieved. This is hereby declared." ▲Telegram from the Eighth Branch of the Sixth District: Briefly states, "Knowing that comrades will use the relics of the 18th century, the hypocritical fallacy of 'courtesy and concession as the way to govern the country,' to invite Chairman Chiang to step down together, and mistakenly quote the saying 'it is better to stop the chaos than to quell the chaos,' if the comrades are not willingly abandoning themselves to the Party, there would be no such absurdity. Because Chairman Chiang is entrusted by the people of the whole country and bears the heavy responsibility of the Party and the country, he has no freedom and the right to leave or stay. It is in the hands of our compatriots across the country. Who are the comrades? Just a public official of the same country. How can one use one's own intentions to violate the public opinion of the people across the country and invite Chairman Chiang to step down together? This is the first absurdity. Is there anyone more foolish than the comrades? Moreover, today, when traitors are lurking and thinking about delaying, the government's only major responsibility is to quell the chaos. Otherwise, the rebellion of Feng Tang, Zhang Li, and other rebels can never overthrow the Party and the country and do whatever they want, plunging us into deep waters. Taking a step back, if it is as the comrades say, 'it is better to stop the chaos than to quell the chaos,' then the comrades should ask themselves whether they have this courage. This error in thinking, is there anything more than the comrades? Comrades, adhering to the spirit of leniency advocated by the late Premier, especially telegraphed exhortations, hoping to realize and wake up, correct the past and start anew, work hard for the Party, and serve the country. News of the National Anti-Drug Campaign

▲Zhejiang Province Takes the Lead: ▲Various Provinces are Preparing: The National Anti-Drug Campaign was initiated by the China National Anti-Drug Association in the spring of the 18th year. An organizing tour group was formed to conduct the anti-drug campaign in accordance with the prescribed locations. The 5th Annual Meeting of the Parliament last year resolved to expand the campaign. The association believes that Jiangsu and Zhejiang are key areas in the country, and the tour campaign should start in these two provinces. A notice was sent to the anti-drug branches of the province to handle the matter conscientiously. It is heard that Zhejiang Province has made preparations and the opening ceremony will be held in Hangzhou on the 26th of this month. On March 1st, the tour will depart from the three prefectures and twenty counties of Hangzhou, Jiaxing, and Huzhou to hold anti-drug meetings in each county. Ji Shiying, a cadre sent to assist in the preparations, has returned after the tour in Zhejiang Province and will go to Jiangsu in the next few days. According to Ji, in addition to the provincial branch sending personnel to lead the tour group organized by the branch, the provincial party department and the civil affairs hall have expressed great sympathy for the campaign and have issued orders to party and administrative organs at all levels to provide concrete assistance, so that the campaign will be popularized throughout the province. Other provinces are also starting to prepare in order to hold the campaign as soon as possible.

Municipal Government to Build Low-Cost Housing in the North and South Districts

The municipal government has built one hundred low-cost houses near Quan Jia An Road in Zhabei, and the operation is considered relatively complete. However, the number is limited and unable to accommodate as many residents as possible. It is necessary to add more. However, there is no low-cost housing in the Nanshi area, and the construction cannot be delayed. Municipal Public Utilities Bureau

Punishes Overloaded Cargo Trucks: The Municipal Public Utilities Bureau believes that overloading trucks not only damages roads but also easily causes danger. It has issued announcements prohibiting overloading and has strictly stipulated clauses in the regulations for punishing vehicles. Violators will be punished according to the regulations without any leniency. The bureau's vehicle inspectors recently discovered two cargo trucks overloading in Nanshi, one belonging to Zhang Yunjia and the other belonging to the Aiwen Automobile Company. The former was loaded with forty pigs and thirty workers, exceeding the specified weight limit by approximately 650 kilograms, and should be fined 32 yuan according to regulations. The latter was loaded with sixty-four pigs and thirty-four workers, exceeding the specified weight limit by approximately 1,600 kilograms, and should be fined 86 yuan according to regulations. Later, the vehicle owners requested leniency in the punishment, but the bureau stated that the regulations were announced and implemented by the municipal government and could not be changed. They were rejected and required to pay the fines within three days.

Public Utilities Bureau Issues Electrical Equipment Inspection Certificates for Public Places

The Municipal Public Utilities Bureau inspects the electrical equipment of public places in the city as soon as new installations are reported, and the existing ones are inspected in districts in sequence. The work is nearing completion. However, after the electrical equipment of these users has passed the inspection, it is difficult to identify it without a proper mark. The bureau has specially produced a "Electrical Equipment Inspection Qualification Certificate for Public Places" and has stipulated seven measures, which have been announced and implemented.

Migration Requires Submission of Rent Book for Verification

▲New Plan to Promote Rent Books: The Shanghai Special Finance Bureau issued a "Rent Book" last year, which was purchased by landlords in the city. Each book is priced at ten cents.

Landlords use it to collect rent from tenants. The bureau also sent a letter to the court stating that in the future, in cases of rent disputes between landlords and tenants, the rent book must be submitted for verification, otherwise the case will not be accepted. Later, the bureau found that the number of rent books sold since the issuance last year has been unsatisfactory. According to statistics, less than a quarter of the households in the city have purchased them. It is clear that landlords are waiting to see what happens. If strict measures are not taken, it will greatly hinder the city's revenue. It has now been decided that in the future, when residents in each district report migration or immigration, they should be required to submit the rent book for verification, otherwise registration will not be allowed. Yesterday, a special letter was sent to the Municipal Public Security Bureau to order the heads and police of household registration in each district to follow the procedures.

Port Authority Rejects

Dada's Request to Maintain Coastline Contract: Dada Steamship Company recently submitted a presentation to the Municipal Port Authority, requesting to maintain the original contract because the company's lease contract for the coastline was announced by the Municipal Port Authority. According to the information, the Port Authority, in accordance with the notice issued by the Municipal Government in November of the 16th year of the Republic of China that all contracts signed between municipal agencies and merchants should be submitted to the government for review. The Contract Review Committee decided that all contracts should be revised and were approved by the Municipal Government, directing the company to comply with the order to submit the original lease contract for the coastline to the government for revision. Since the establishment of the Port Authority, the company has delayed the matter for more than two years, citing various excuses. The company is both violating the order and abandoning its rights. The municipal government should adhere to the principle of developing the social economy when promoting local undertakings. The company's pursuit of profit and monopoly has caused suffering to ship merchants, hindering the progress of shipping. To declare the company's original coastline contract invalid and to take back the wharf built by the city is a proper administrative action. However, in order to show consideration for the merchants' difficulties, the committee was established to evaluate the price of the wharf and other buildings, and pay for the recovery, which is in the development of the social economy, while maintaining the interests of merchants. The Port Authority has rejected the request.

Municipal Bureau of Social Affairs

Restricts Short-Term Employment Contracts: The Shanghai Silk Weaving Factory of Weicheng Company recently leased its factory cheaply due to its inability to maintain operations, and signed employment contracts with workers for only three months. The Bureau of Social Affairs' Investigation Office learned of this and immediately ordered a correction and informed the trade union. It also instructed the Electrical Machinery Silk Weaving Industry Association to prohibit similar situations. The instructions stated: "For compliance matters, the 50th Bureau Affairs Meeting of this Bureau decided that the minimum term of employment contracts should be one year. Now, according to the investigation report, the Shanghai Silk Weaving Factory of Weicheng Company rented out the entire factory due to its inability to maintain operations and signed employment contracts with workers for only three months, etc. Therefore, in addition to ordering corrections, we urge you to inform the industry to comply."

Electricity

Instructions Regarding the Revision of Wage Standards for the Silk Weaving Industry ▲ Must Comply with and Implement Labor Agreement Conditions ▲ The Shanghai Electrical Silk Weaving Trade Association, citing the increasing number of independent weaving machines in the city—investigations reveal over 4,000, more than double the number in the association's factories—reported that the wages of these independent machines are unrestricted and that there is no set method for their sale. The majority are sold wholesale by shops or door-to-door. Due to lower costs, they are easily marketed. At a time when sales are sluggish and business is plummeting, this formidable competition makes it difficult to cope without reducing wages to compete. Therefore, they have repeatedly petitioned the Social Affairs Bureau for permission to revise wages as a remedy. An investigation by the Social Affairs Bureau found that the wage provisions in the labor-management agreement for the industry were quite appropriate. The current situation is entirely due to factories in the industry freely increasing production during good business times, leading to unlimited growth. The Social Affairs Bureau immediately issued an order to the association, instructing them to inform their members to comply with and implement the conditions uniformly. The original text of the instructions is recorded below. Both submissions have been noted. Upon review of the wage standards for various goods, Article 3 of the labor-management agreed treatment conditions for the industry already provides specific regulations. It is hereby ordered that the association notify its members to comply with and implement them uniformly. This concludes the instructions.

Strictly Prohibit Counterfeit Stamp Tax Tickets

Stamp tax tickets have always been produced under the supervision of the Ministry of Finance. Current criminal law stipulates strict penalties for counterfeiting. The Ministry of Finance has repeatedly issued announcements and orders to prevent counterfeiting. It has been reported that the Jiangsu Stamp Tax Bureau recently received an order from the Ministry of Finance, fearing that negligence may occur over time, instructing them to reissue an announcement of the penal articles. The original text of the announcement is recorded below: Regarding the matter of the announcement, an order was received from the Ministry of Finance stating: "Upon investigation, stamp tax tickets are produced under the supervision of the Ministry. Counterfeiting or altering [them] is subject to criminal penalties under current criminal law." Furthermore, the Ministry has repeatedly issued announcements and orders to prevent [such acts], issuing repeated instructions. However, fearing that negligence may arise over time and that ignorant commoners may not fully understand the penal statutes, leading to them being caught in the web of the law, which is pitiable, we hereby specifically transcribe the articles of the criminal law concerning the penalties for counterfeiting and altering, for strict prohibition. The bureau is instructed to promptly announce this to the provinces under its jurisdiction to ensure widespread knowledge, so that all may be warned and not test the law. It is also instructed to thoroughly investigate and prohibit [such acts] to uphold the law and emphasize tax policy. In addition, an excerpt of the articles of the criminal law is attached." Upon receiving this order, in addition to instructing all subordinate bureaus to thoroughly investigate and prohibit [such acts], this bureau is compelled to record the articles of the criminal law below and announce them to merchants and commoners, informing them that counterfeiting or altering stamps is an illegal act, and offenders will be punished without leniency. Once discovered, they will be severely dealt with according to the law. Exercise caution and do not bring trouble upon yourselves. Everyone must strictly comply and not neglect. This is imperative. This announcement. The included Chapter 14 of the Criminal Law, Crimes of Forging Documents and Seals, concerning the penal articles for counterfeiting or altering stamp tax tickets: Article 227 of the Criminal Law: "Anyone who, with the intent to provide for use, counterfeits or alters postage stamps and various stamp tax tickets issued by the government, shall be sentenced to imprisonment for not less than six months and not more than five years, and may also be fined not more than one thousand yuan." "Anyone who, with the intent to provide for use, collects counterfeit or altered postage stamps and various stamp tax tickets issued by the government, shall be subject to the same penalty." "Anyone who, with the intent to provide for use, defaces the cancellation marks on postage stamps and various stamp tax tickets issued by the government shall be considered to have counterfeited [them]." Article 233: "Anyone who uses documents under Articles 224 to 232 shall be punished according to the regulations on forging or altering documents or entering indefinite matters or causing false matters to be entered." "Anyone who uses already used postage stamps and various stamp tax tickets issued by the government shall be considered to have used counterfeit postage stamps or stamp tax tickets." "Attempted crimes under this article shall be punished." Article 236: "Anyone who, with the intent to provide for the use of counterfeiting or altering valuable securities, postage stamps, and various stamp tax tickets issued by the government, manufactures, delivers, or receives various instruments or raw materials, shall be sentenced to imprisonment for not more than two years, and may also be fined not more than five hundred yuan." Article 237: "Valuable securities, postage stamps, various stamp tax tickets issued by the government, seals, and the instruments and raw materials mentioned in the preceding article that have been counterfeited or altered, regardless of whether they belong to the offender, shall be confiscated." Article 239: "Anyone who commits a crime under this chapter may be deprived of public rights in accordance with the provisions of Articles 57 and 58."

Do not delay. This order.'" The following resolutions were made: (A) In accordance with the letter, the name "Shanghai Special City Silk and Satin Trade Association" would be used; (B) In accordance with the order, the old name would be abolished immediately, and the association would exercise its powers under the name of the Trade Association; (C) The articles of association of the Trade Association would be drafted, and Wang Yansong, Luo Qinghua, Zhang Hongsun, Lu Zhengbing, and Jiang Linshu would be appointed as drafting committee members, with Luo Qinghua responsible for convening the meeting. The Reality of Silver Transport Bidding

The transportation of silver dollars in Shanghai has traditionally been undertaken by the Datong Xinji Transportation Company of Ningbo Road Tonghe Lane. Later, due to the Ministry of Railways increasing freight rates and the discount given to the company being reduced from 28% to 15%, and since the burning of the Nanjing Mint resulted in no large amounts of silver coins to transport, and the Central Bank needed to transport silver for free, business declined sharply, making it impossible to maintain operations. At the end of last year according to the lunar calendar, the company sent a letter to the Silver Trade Association and the Money Trade Association stating that it would cease transportation services starting in January of this year. Since the company stopped operating, whenever silver dollars needed to be transported in or out, personnel had to be sent to liaise with the station in person and to escort the shipment, which was not only costly and cumbersome but also raised concerns about accidents. It was hoped that the Ministry of Railways would invite bids for a contractor. The bidding was originally scheduled to take place on the 14th of this month, so that someone would be responsible for the transportation from then on. However, all transportation companies believed that even with 28%, they would still lose money, so there was no way to reduce the discount. As a result, no one dared to bid, and no one is responsible for transportation to this day. The Silver Trade Association believes that this is a major issue, and the spring silkworm season is approaching, creating a need for silver transport.

Continuing this delay is highly inappropriate. It is now planned to detail the difficult situation to the Ministry of Railways and request assistance.

Shanghai Citizen Training Committee Forbids Staff from Receiving Entertainment

▲Strict Penalties Established in Three Articles ▲ To Prevent Solicitation from Both Labor and Management ▲ The Municipal Party Committee's Mass Training Committee recently noted that when disputes occasionally arise between labor and management in the city, banquets are often hosted to entertain the committee's staff in the hope of gaining influence. The committee deemed this inappropriate and, after a resolution at the tenth standing committee meeting, has banned staff members from accepting entertainment when disputes arise between labor and management, and has instructed the district mass training directors to report to the executive committee for record. The order to the district mass training directors is recorded below: Regarding the matter of the notification, it has been noted that when disputes occur between labor and management in the city, staff members of this committee are invited to banquets to explain the case or even to solicit favors in order to obtain convenience. Such a situation easily creates a pretext for criticism. After deliberation at the tenth meeting of this committee, it has been decided that if any staff member of the committee is found to have engaged in the above-mentioned conduct, they will be penalized as follows: the first offense will result in a fine of half a month's salary, the second offense will result in suspension of duties for one month, and the third offense will result in dismissal from employment. This matter concerns the rectification of internal staff and has been reported to the Municipal Executive Committee for review and record. You are hereby ordered to notify your staff accordingly. This order.
